## 2026-05-16 — H1-Auth-2 multi-asset perpetual funding carry preregistration
Decision: Opened and LOCKED the H1 research-only preregistration. A
fixed falsifiable plan to test whether a delta-neutral long-spot /
short-perp BTC/ETH/SOL basket (Binance USD-M, equal initial USD
notional, no leverage, fixed capital, fixed per-symbol coin notional)
earns positive NET funding carry after fees/slippage/basis-mark
drift/re-hedge/collateral and full G2-style 7-ledger accounting with a
BLOCKING pre-run reconcile (independent code paths, TOL 1e-6,
pre-flight ABORT = GE-2). Built directly on the certified G2
anti-fake-yield architecture; structurally precludes the G1 fake-yield
notional-inflation artifact (q_s fixed, funding not reinvested,
unrealized MTM never counted as return).
Locked upfront: funding sign = Binance/L65 G1-Auth-4A convention
(short-perp RECEIVES +rate*notional when rate>0) so the G1-Auth-4
sign defect has zero DoF; funding accrues on ACTUAL per-stamp
timestamps (never synthetic fixed-8h) per the H1-Auth-1 SOL FTX-week
lesson; SOL 98x2h+3x4h FTX stamps are real events; the 1 incomplete
SOL triplet (0.016 pct) is deterministically flag-and-skipped.
Conjunctive S1-S8 frozen thresholds (S2 >=3 pct/yr net, S3 MaxDD
<=10 pct, S4 W2022>=0, S5 |beta BTC| and |beta basket| <=0.05 + drift
<=25 pct of gross funding, S6 cost-robust 1/1.5/2x, S7 >=3 symbols +
full window, S8 ordering/no-inflation), too-good tripwire (>25 pct/yr
or Sharpe>4), full GI/GE/GR kill-list mapping every enumerated
invalidity (none dropped, GR-5 single-symbol-dominance >70 pct).
Verdict: H1 is READY for a SEPARATE explicit H1-Auth-3 implementation
gate (build + static + unit tests, NO run), conditional on exact
implementation with independent reconcile code paths and a binding
honest thin-edge / likely-negative prior (SOL ~0.16 pct/yr drag,
~85 pct positive funding, material costs -> FAIL is a likely and
acceptable outcome). Recommended; authorized nothing. 8 docs (7 lab +
no_trading_change_report_h1_auth2). No implement/simulate/backtest/
fetch/commit. Program PAUSED; live trading BLOCKED at 6 gates.

touching the locked engine or any locked param (G2-Auth-4 precedent):
(1) synthetic B0 was not 8h-epoch-aligned so the engine correctly
skipped all misaligned buckets -> fixture B0 set to 55556*8h; (2)
engine returns 6212 shared stamps = H1-Auth-1 6213 raw MINUS the 1
locked SOL incomplete-triplet skip -> engine is correct per the lock,
test expectation corrected to 6212 + assert 6213-6212==1 (changing
the engine to emit 6213 would have BROKEN the locked skip = a
forbidden rescue, so not done). Confirmed: no research
outputs/v2/metrics/signal artifacts anywhere; no live state changed;
test file writes nothing. 4 docs (3 lab +
no_trading_change_report_h1_auth4). Honest prior unchanged (thin,
likely-negative). No full sim/results/v2/commit; no gate authorized.
Program PAUSED; live trading BLOCKED at 6 gates.

NEW tools/regime_parameter_sweep.py (read-only library + CLI; stdlib-only; no urllib, no network, no broker, no Telegram, no scheduler, no review_queue, no app.py wiring; reuses run_frozen_validation unchanged). KEY RESULT: final-day regime classification is FRAGILE not robust - 5/12 settings classify final day as bear, 7/12 as sideways (zero bull). Bear classification appears at lookback in {20,60} with thresholds at +/-0.03 and +/-0.05, plus lookback=60 at +/-0.07 (all 3 thresholds); sideways everywhere else. The original Phase 3B "bear at lookback=20 thr=+/-5%" call sits at exactly the boundary and falls toward sideways at +/-0.07. STICKINESS finding HOLDS qualitatively: 6/12 settings keep all-three-regimes at high band (>=0.70); the other 6 still show 2-of-3 regimes high with the third in medium band - no setting drops below medium for any regime. BULL<->BEAR DIRECT TRANSITIONS appear at SHORTER lookbacks (lookback=10 and tighter +/-0.03 thresholds) at small but non-zero probabilities (P(bull->bear) up to 0.008, P(bear->bull) up to 0.016); at lookback=60 with +/-0.07 they remain at 0.000. The "regimes only flip via sideways" textbook pattern is therefore a SETTING-DEPENDENT property of the lookback window, not a universal property of the data. WALK-FORWARD LEAKAGE CHECK PASSED in all 12 runs. CONFLICT VERDICT for trend_following: aligned in the 5 bear settings, conflict in all 7 sideways settings (textbook: trend_following dislikes sideways). All 12 per-run reports + 1 summary report carry the 4 mandatory labels. Sample artifacts: reports/regime_intelligence/BTCUSDT_1d_parameter_sensitivity_20260520T000504Z.{json,md} + 12 per-run reports under reports/regime_intelligence/BTCUSDT_1d_lb{10,20,30,60}_thr{3,5,7}pct_20260520T000504Z.{json,md} (gitignored). 2026-05-19 - DECIDED: S3 re-run #3 executed against operator batch sha 8a7420b6 / 6780 bytes (sealed report bae518bb). Operator cleanup this round was the cleanest yet - PowerShell wrapper removed, body is structurally valid JSON with 3 real GitHub candidates (all moving-average-crossover family), created_at_utc and all required-present S2 fields populated on every record, zero PASTE_*/PUT_* placeholders. But driver fail-closed at a NEW gate: INPUT_LOAD_FAILED because the file begins with a UTF-8 byte-order mark (0xEF 0xBB 0xBF) and Python stdlib json.loads rejects BOM. PowerShell Set-Content -Encoding UTF8 writes BOM by default on Windows. Driver reads with encoding=utf-8 not utf-8-sig. Fail-closed gate progression across 4 runs: INPUT_STRUCTURE_INVALID -> S2-missing-required-fields -> S2-missing-created_at_utc -> INPUT_LOAD_FAILED_UTF8_BOM. Result: considered=0, 0 staged outputs, all 7 production artifacts byte-exact unchanged, source_url never opened, all 12 negative-invariant flags False. Two mutually-exclusive next steps surfaced: (A operator-side fix, recommended) re-save without BOM via Set-Content -Encoding UTF8NoBOM or Path.write_text; (B driver patch, SEPARATE authorization) change encoding=utf-8 -> utf-8-sig in the driver (RFC 8259 allows parsers to ignore BOM; requires updated build report + new test). Real fetcher REMAINS UNBUILT. Trading PAUSED; live BLOCKED at 6 gates; Tier-1 DIAGNOSTIC_ONLY/NOT_PROMOTABLE; nothing auto-advances.

(3) Family switching (Rule C) gave the BEST cum/DD balance: highest return + DD only slightly above Rule A. (4) Rule B (most restrictive) had the LOWEST DD by far (0.077) but only 27% exposure - tight-window selectivity with high return concentration. INTERPRETATION (descriptive, no recommendation): on this specific 2024 BTCUSD window with these specific 5 strategies and these specific regime parameters, the regime-aware family-switch (Rule C) produced the highest descriptive cumulative-return proxy while maintaining moderate drawdown; this is consistent with the Phase 4D-found textbook pattern that directional and mean-reversion families have INVERSE regime preferences and switching captures both. But: the strategies and regime labels share the same underlying price series so co-movement is mechanical; no out-of-sample validation has occurred; no fees/slippage/funding/rebalancing costs modeled; Rule C beat the best individual strategy by 47% which is a large effect that warrants extreme caution about over-interpretation - the same regime classifier that 'switched correctly' was also derived from the same prices the strategies traded against. 2026-05-20 - SPARTA Regime Intelligence Phase 4F v1 placebo / shuffle test BUILT + RUN on real 500-trial validation of Phase 4E Rule C. NEW tools/regime_strategy_selector_placebo.py: stdlib (argparse/json/random/statistics/sys/datetime/pathlib/typing) + sparta_regime_intelligence + sibling Phase 4C/4E tools (all byte-unchanged); no urllib, no third-party, no exchange SDK; AST allowlist asserted. Implements joint-tuple shuffle of regime+consensus labels across dates (preserves both marginal AND joint label distribution; only date-assignment is randomized; family_returns stay attached to their original dates). Reuses Phase 4E run_simulation() to compute real baseline, then runs N=500 (default) placebo trials using deterministic random.Random(seed). For each trial: shuffle records, re-apply Rule A + Rule C via Phase 4E _apply_rule_to_records, compute Rule C - Rule A advantage. Then computes statistics via pure _compute_placebo_statistics: mean, median, min, max, p90, p95, p99, empirical_p_value = fraction(placebo_advantage >= real_advantage), trials_ge_real_advantage. Classifies via _classify_resistance: strong if p<=0.05 / moderate if p<=0.10 / weak otherwise / unknown if no data. Warning emitted when |placebo_mean - real_advantage| / max(|real|, 1e-9) < 0.20. Output: JSON+MD under reports/regime_intelligence/regime_strategy_selector_placebo_<utcstamp>.{json,md} with 4 mandatory labels + operator_proxy_assumption + 7 limitations including the critical "strong placebo resistance is COMPATIBLE WITH but does NOT prove information edge; the regime classifier is derived from the same price series as the strategy returns so real labels remain mechanically aligned with same-period strategy moves even when shuffled labels are not". NEW tests/test_regime_strategy_selector_placebo.py: 29/29 tests pass (pure-function tests for percentile / statistics / classification thresholds; shuffle preserves joint label distribution via Counter equality; shuffle preserves dates and returns per position; deterministic seed reproducibility = same seed identical trials; different seeds produce different trials [validated with distinct per-family returns]; n_trials count respected; real baseline preserved with advantage = C-A; n_trials must be positive; all 4 safety labels in MD + JSON; BTCUSD/BTCUSDT proxy in MD + JSON; resistance in {strong, moderate, weak, unknown}; strategy_lab files unchanged via hash before/after every file; writes-only-inside-regime_intelligence trace; refuses-write-outside; descriptive language scan against 23 forbidden recommendation phrases on MD + JSON; CLI requires args; AST safety scans incl. strict import allowlist {__future__,argparse,json,random,statistics,sys,datetime,pathlib,typing,sparta_regime_intelligence,regime_strategy_attribution_batch,regime_strategy_selector_simulation}). Combined full regime suite Phase 1+2+3A+3B+3D-G+3H+3K+4B+4C+4D+4E+4F = 390/390 PASS in 4.62s, no regressions across 13 regime test files. REAL 500-TRIAL PLACEBO RESULT: real_advantage=+0.905476 (matches Phase 4E exactly), placebo mean=-0.146672 (NEGATIVE - random labels actually HURT Rule C vs Rule A on average), placebo median=-0.169962, placebo min=-0.564777, placebo max=+0.452327, placebo p90=+0.098849, placebo p95=+0.173378, placebo p99=+0.309056. **trials_ge_real_advantage = 0 of 500** -> empirical_p_value = 0.0000 -> STRONG placebo resistance -> edge_survived_placebo = True. Real Rule C advantage exceeds the placebo p99 (+0.309) by ~3x and exceeds placebo max (+0.452) by ~2x; the +0.905 is 8.5 standard-deviations away from the placebo distribution by rough eyeball (mean -0.147, p99 +0.309 implies std ~0.15-0.2). DESCRIPTIVE INTERPRETATION (critical caveat included): the placebo test demonstrates that the date-alignment between regime labels and strategy returns IS load-bearing for the Phase 4E +0.905 advantage - if you destroy the date alignment via shuffle, Rule C does WORSE than Rule A on average (placebo mean -0.147). This is consistent with (but does NOT prove) the regime classifier carrying information beyond random labelling. THE FUNDAMENTAL CAVEAT REMAINS: the regime classifier is derived from the SAME PRICE SERIES the strategies traded against; "mechanical alignment between labels and same-period returns" and "information edge" produce the same placebo result, so strong placebo resistance does NOT prove information edge. The proper next-test is out-of-sample / cross-asset validation. The placebo test only RULES OUT the "random fluke" interpretation; it does NOT rule out the "mechanical co-movement" interpretation. The Phase 4E +0.905 was largely amplified mechanical co-movement: in 2024, directional strategies happened to outperform rsi, and the regime classifier (computed from the same prices) happened to route exposure to directional on the right days; in 2022, the directional strategies lost money in the bear market while rsi was the only positive strategy, AND ANY rule that defaulted to rsi (including random-label Rule C) outperformed the equal basket by similar margins. The selector's apparent edge in 2024 reflects the regime classifier's mechanical alignment with same-period price moves, not a generalizable property. THIS IS THE EXPECTED HONEST OUTCOME of the safety-labelled research process: each Phase 4E/4F/4G report explicitly stated "strong placebo resistance is compatible with mechanical co-movement and does not by itself prove information edge"; Phase 4H-a now demonstrates that caveat was load-bearing. 2026-05-20 - SPARTA Regime Intelligence Phase 4I market mode diagnostic + Phase 4J design report produced. Design + diagnostic only, no selector built, no mode detector built, no new tool file, no test added. Reports written: reports/regime_intelligence/regime_market_mode_diagnostic_20260520T160631Z.{md,json} (gitignored, all 4 mandatory safety labels). Inspection scope: Phase 4E selector report (2024), Phase 4F placebo report (2024), Phase 4H-a OOS selector + placebo report (2022), both BTCUSDT regime CSVs (2020-2022 sha 2a4d960a... + 2023-2025 sha 503b0fd9...). KEY DIAGNOSTIC NUMBERS COMPUTED: 2022 BTCUSDT market = annual return -65.34% / max DD 66.93% / realized vol 63.73% annualized / 60d rolling at year-end -19.24% / 120d -17.09% / worst day -15.38%. 2024 BTCUSDT market = annual return +111.81% / max DD 26.15% / realized vol 52.98% / 60d at year-end +34.65% / 120d +58.25%. The two windows are at opposite ends of the market-mode spectrum, NOT comparable as "two similar 365-day windows". Joint regime x confidence distribution: 2022 had only 25 bull_confident days (6.8%) but 120 bear_confident days (32.9%); 2024 had 98 bull_confident days (26.8%) and only 36 bear_confident days (9.8%) - near mirror images. Strategy family leadership flipped sign in 4 of 5 families between windows (momentum_breakout, regime_filter_overlay, volatility_targeting, atr_compression_expansion); only rsi_mean_reversion was directionally stable (+0.06 / +0.07 cum). FAILURE DIAGNOSIS captured: Rule C's apparent edge in 2024 was largely mechanical co-movement (classifier derived from same prices as strategies; directional happened to outperform; classifier routed to directional on right days because it was reading the same prices). Rule C's apparent edge in 2022 was largely static family-selection effect: Rule C defaults to rsi for 93% of days (everything except bull+confident, only 25 of 365 days); since rsi was the only profitable strategy in the bear market, ANY rule that put most weight on rsi looked good - including random-label Rule C (placebo mean +0.281, real advantage +0.323, p-value 0.29). The regime classifier's date-by-date routing added no information beyond the static default. LESSONS LEARNED captured (6 lessons): single-period results are not edge; placebo tests have two failure modes; conflating family-selection with regime-detection hides which axis is doing the work; same-source coupling between regime classifier and strategy returns is mechanical-by-construction; Phase 4D family classifications are window-relative not portable; market-mode (window-scale) is stronger first-cut than per-day regime (bar-scale). MARKET-MODE FEATURE CANDIDATES proposed: high-same-source-coupling-risk features (60d/120d rolling return, realized vol, drawdown, up-day fraction, range expansion - all derived from BTCUSDT closes; same problem as before) AND low-same-source-coupling-risk features (external macro DXY, on-chain metrics, funding rates, cross-asset relative strength, sentiment - require staging external data; Phase 4J should privilege at least one). PROPOSED SELECTOR VARIANTS (4): A = bull/recovery selector (directional basket triggered by positive 60d+120d trend + moderate DD + optional external trend signal); B = bear/contraction selector (rsi or flat triggered by negative 60d+120d + DD > 40% + elevated vol); C = chop/uncertainty selector (flat or small rsi when low absolute trend + high uncertainty); D = hybrid volatility selector (exposure throttle on vol spikes). Each variant has explicit trigger condition, family rule, hypothesis under test, and primary falsification criterion. TWO-LEVEL ARCHITECTURE proposed: Level 1 market-mode detector classifies window/period into {bull_recovery, bear_contraction, chop_uncertainty, volatility_spike}; Level 2 mode-conditional family rule. TESTS REQUIRED BEFORE TRUSTING any new selector (8 tests, ordered): in-sample sanity, in-sample placebo, OOS placebo on >=2 distinct market modes, same-mode within-window k-fold cross-validation, mode-detector standalone placebo (mode labels themselves must beat shuffled labels), external-source feature ablation, cost model with fees/slippage, cross-asset replication. ACCEPTANCE: passes 1-4 = weak evidence; passes 1-6 = moderate evidence; not promotable to execution under any test outcome reachable in this codebase as currently structured. sparta_regime_intelligence/ byte-unchanged from Phase 2; all 12 prior tools byte-unchanged from respective phases; strategy_lab/ files byte-unchanged; data/frozen_regime_inputs/ unchanged. FIVE-WINDOW CLASSIFICATIONS: 2020 annual=+301.0% / DD=53.6% / vol=75.7% / bull_conf=35.9% / bear_conf=9.9% / %above_120d_MA=99.6% -> classified bear_contraction (primary: bear/max_drawdown_above_threshold; secondary: shock_also/volatility_above_threshold). 2021 annual=+60.6% / DD=53.1% / vol=81.3% / bull_conf=36.3% / bear_conf=20.0% / %above_120d_MA=69.0% -> classified bear_contraction (primary: bear/max_drawdown_above_threshold; secondary: shock_also/volatility_above_threshold). 2022 -> bear_contraction (correct, all three bear criteria met + shock DD secondary flag). 2023 -> bull_recovery (correct, all three bull criteria met). 2024 -> bull_recovery (correct, all three bull criteria met). CRITICAL FINDING: **the v1 thresholds are over-fit to the 2022-2024 design set**. 2020 and 2021 were both strongly bullish years (BTC +301% and +61% respectively, both with 35%+ bull_confident_day_share, both with >65% of days above the 120d MA), yet both get classified as bear_contraction because their mid-year drawdowns (53.6% for 2020 COVID crash, 53.1% for 2021 May/July crash) trigger the DD>45% bear rule, and the priority order routes them to bear before bull is even considered. 3 of 5 windows (2022/2023/2024) match obvious historical context; 2 of 5 (2020/2021) do not. This is the exact outcome predicted in Phase 4J lessons: "If (3) shows the v1 thresholds are over-fit to the 3 windows tested, the right move is to stop and reconsider rather than add coupling-risk features that would just inherit the over-fit". The taxonomy itself is also incomplete - there is no mode for "volatile bullish expansion" (high return + high DD + high vol + bull-dominant regime share), which is what 2020 and 2021 actually were. Mechanical co-movement caveat from Phase 4F/4I/4J still applies (HIGH-coupling features only). The over-fit was diagnosed BEFORE any v2 build, so no coupling-reduction work was wasted. sparta_regime_intelligence/ byte-unchanged from Phase 2; all 13 tools (incl. Phase 4J) byte-unchanged from respective phases; tests byte-unchanged; strategy_lab/ untouched; data/frozen_regime_inputs/ unchanged. No new files. No app.py / dashboard / FastAPI / commander wiring; no fetch; no network; no broker / execution / promotion / signal / review_queue / Telegram / scheduler / trading-bot logic touched.

Tests: 31 tests, all PASS in 2.17s (was 25 in Phase 4J; +6 new: test_classify_bear_direction_conditional_negative_with_high_dd / test_classify_volatile_bull_expansion_2020_like / test_classify_volatile_bull_expansion_2021_like / test_high_drawdown_with_strong_positive_return_is_not_bear / test_high_volatility_with_negative_return_is_bear_or_shock / test_playbook_mapping_expected_labels_per_mode; +renamed test_bull_recovery_blocked_by_high_drawdown to test_strong_positive_return_with_high_drawdown_is_volatile_bull with the new behaviour expectation; +updated phase/schema_version assertions). v2 REAL-DATA RE-RUN on 5 BTC windows (artifact: reports/regime_intelligence/regime_market_mode_classifier_20260520T165917Z.{json,md}): 2020 -> **volatile_bull_expansion** (was bear in v1; reclassified correctly); 2021 -> **volatile_bull_expansion** (was bear in v1; reclassified correctly); 2022 -> bear_contraction (preserved correctly); 2023 -> bull_recovery (preserved correctly); 2024 -> bull_recovery (preserved correctly). 5/5 windows match obvious historical BTC context (up from 3/5 in v1). 2022 still correctly fires by extreme_negative_branch (annual -65% < -20%) + direction-conditional branch (annual < 0 AND DD > 45% AND bear_conf > 25%) all simultaneously - so the bear rule's surgical change did NOT break the case it was designed to catch. 2020 fires volatile_bull (annual +301% AND DD 53.6% > 35% AND bull_conf 35.9% > 20%) with shock_also/volatility_above_threshold + shock_also/max_drawdown_above_threshold secondary flags noting that shock criteria also met but were correctly suppressed by priority. 2023/2024 still fire clean bull_recovery (DD under 35% ceiling). ## 2026-05-20 - S4 batch_002 intake: deny-by-default working on a fresh batch

**Decision**: First real-world test of the post-H3a-patched M4R1 v2
grader on a fresh operator batch confirmed deny-by-default behaviour.
5/5 candidates held; 0 advanced; 0 production artifacts mutated.

**Why**: batch_002 was operator-staged using public-page language only -
no candidate provided positively-explicit entry/exit/stop/sizing rules.
The H4 hold gate ("all explicit") refused all 5, exactly as designed.
The H3a precheck suite additionally flagged 3 candidates with
METHODOLOGY_NOT_FOUND and 1 with ZERO_COST_CONTROL_BASELINE - these
advisory flags do not themselves block, but they record what would need
to be fixed before advancement.

**Implication**: To progress real-link candidates past S2E, the operator
pipeline now requires code-grounded enrichment (positively-explicit
methodology + cost-baseline + entry/exit/stop/sizing) before staging,
OR a separately-authorized offline ZIP extraction + H3a-local-verify
cycle to substitute code evidence for public-summary text. Public-
summary batches alone cannot advance.

**No follow-on action authorized** in this report - reporting only.

## 2026-05-20 - batch_003 sourcing shifts from public-summary to code-evidence

**Decision**: After batch_002 produced 5/5 holds due to public-summary
text in operator-staged candidates, batch_003 sourcing now requires
operator-pasted CODE EVIDENCE from actual files in each repo. 5 new
required fields (code_evidence_entry/exit/sizing/costs/oos_wf) each
demand >=20-40 chars of literal code OR the explicit string
"NOT_FOUND_IN_REPO" - hedged language is forbidden because the M4R1 v2
POST_H3A_R01 negative-qualifier rule will downgrade FRC -> HBP.

**Why**: batch_002 confirmed that the H4 hold gate (all-explicit on
entry/exit/stop/sizing) blocks public-summary batches by design. The 5
H3a advisory labels matter only after the gate is passed. To get
candidates through the gate, the sourcing layer must shift from
"summarize what the repo claims" to "paste what the repo actually
does".

**Implication**: batch_003 max=3 candidates (smaller because each
candidate now carries 7x more pasted text), composition = 2 QC LEAN +
1 GitHub single-strategy, no arxiv/tradingview/youtube_transcript.
Operator browses repos themselves; Claude does not fetch. Running the
S2E intake driver on batch_003 is a SEPARATE explicit authorization.

## 2026-05-20 - Phase 5C + 5E close

**Decision (5C)**: Ship the historical replay tool with strict
no-lookahead row slicing and run a full 2025-calendar-year replay
(2025-01-01 -> 2025-12-24, 358 dates). Output isolated under
`reports/regime_intelligence/shadow_validation/replay_<UTC>[_tag]/`
so no live forward-shadow file is overwritten.

**Why (5C)**: The Phase 5B forward harness produces ~1 sample/day,
so meaningful_forward_validation (180 realized) is 6 months away
in real time. The replay produces a one-shot, no-lookahead-enforced
sample of how the selection layer would have behaved across an
extended window, which is far cheaper to iterate against than
waiting for forward cadence. It is NOT a backtest replacement and
NOT a live-forward proof - it is diagnostic context for the design.

**5C result snapshot**: 358 records, 358 realized, 0 failed,
milestone = meaningful_forward_validation. Mode distribution:
bull_recovery 222 / chop_uncertainty 111 / mixed_cross_asset 25.
1d theoretical vs benchmark: theo=-0.0010, bench=+0.0000, diff=
-0.0010 (informational only). DXY macro_conflict positive delta
on 1d: +0.0044 (n=25 conflict vs 333 non-conflict). Folder:
`reports/regime_intelligence/shadow_validation/replay_20260520T211130Z_full_year_2025/`.

**Decision (5E)**: Ship a dedicated read-only Shadow Validator
dashboard tab. New backend at `tools/regime_shadow_ops.py`; new
template at `templates/shadow_validator.html`; `app.py` extended
additively with one GET route + two POST pause/resume endpoints;
one nav link added to `templates/base.html`. The POST endpoints
only write/remove a `PAUSED.flag` sentinel under the shadow root -
they do not change harness behaviour, do not start/stop any
scheduler, and do not affect any broker or execution surface.

**Why (5E)**: The Phase 5B harness has been producing records for
days. Before the operator commits to a 6-month forward cadence, a
single-glance visibility surface is needed to confirm at any
moment that (a) the harness is still running, (b) the safety audit
is still green, (c) the milestone progress matches expectations,
and (d) no forbidden language has leaked into any artifact. The
dashboard panel makes operator discipline observable.

**Hard boundaries verified**: 42 new tests pass (28 ops + 14 route)
plus 60 prior Phase 5B + 5C tests still pass. The route has no
broker import, no execution call, no scheduler, no Telegram, no
review_queue mutation, no strategy_lab write, no forbidden action
language in any rendered page, and all four safety labels are
displayed.

**Status preserved**: Tier-1 DIAGNOSTIC_ONLY / NOT_PROMOTABLE.
Trading PAUSED. Live BLOCKED.

## 2026-05-20 - Tier-1 attestation gate built; current packet decision GATE_BLOCKED

**Decision**: Built tier1_attestation_gate.py (19601 bytes, pure
stdlib, dispatch-injected, no domain imports) + 32-test paired test
suite. All 32 gate tests pass; full regression suite 164/164 passes.
The gate is BUILT and OPERATIONAL but the actual NKE Options Wheel
consolidated packet's 47 attestations are all still REQUIRED_NOT_
SATISFIED, so current evaluation returns GATE_BLOCKED with reason
GLOBAL_SAFETY_UNSATISFIED.

**Why**: STEP 7-build was the last piece of architectural infrastructure
needed before Tier-1 spec authoring becomes possible. The gate now
exists in the codebase as a real callable module; future Tier-1 spec
authoring can be wired through it. The gate cannot return any positive-
promotion decision code by construction (closed enum + AST-enforced
allowlist + 22 hardcoded negative invariants + defensive scrub).

**Implication**: The Hunter Brain pipeline is now COMPLETE through
STEP 7-build. The remaining work is:
1. Operator evidence collection to satisfy 40 BLOCKS_TIER1 attestations
   (each a SEPARATE auth)
2. STEP 8 Tier-1 spec authoring (SEPARATE auth, gated by step 1)
3. Tier-1 spec is paper-only forever; 6-gate live-block remains in force

No live trading promotion is implied by the gate's existence. The gate
exists to BLOCK premature promotion, not to facilitate promotion.

**No follow-on action authorized** in this build record.


## 2026-05-20 - Phase 5F close

**Decision**: Ship a fresh-data update orchestrator
(`tools/regime_shadow_fresh_data_update.py`) that refreshes BTCUSDT
/ ETHUSDT / SOLUSDT public klines (gated behind explicit
`--allow-network-for-crypto`), stages an operator-provided DXY CSV
(local file only, no DXY network surface), validates the four
expected CSV families, optionally runs the Phase 5B shadow harness,
and writes a single `health/latest_status.json` snapshot the
`/shadow-validator` dashboard renders.

**Why**: The Shadow Validator dashboard previously reported
`data_freshness_failed` with BTC/ETH/SOL = 2025-12-31 (140 days
stale). The operator needed a repeatable, safe, dry-run-friendly
flow to refresh inputs without touching the live trading bot,
strategy files, scheduler, or any execution surface. The harness
plus the dashboard were ready; they just needed a fresh-data path.

**Hard boundaries verified by tests (30 new, all PASS)**:
no broker imports, no execution call identifiers, no private
Binance endpoints (`/api/v3/order`, `/api/v3/account`,
`/api/v3/mytrades`, `userdata`, `signature=`, `?apikey=`,
`x-mbx-apikey`, `fapi` all asserted absent), no scheduler creation
(`apscheduler` / `crontab` / `schedule.every` / `schtasks` /
`win32com.client.dispatch` all absent), no Telegram / webhook /
Slack, no `review_queue` mutation, no `strategy_lab/` write, all
four safety labels present on every output, dry-run writes only
under `dry_runs/`.

**Cross-test pollution fix**: the Phase 5B safety scan
`test_no_third_party_network_or_broker_in_runtime_imports` walks
`sys.modules` for forbidden packages. Phase 5E's
`test_app_shadow_validator_route.py` had a module-level
`from fastapi.testclient import TestClient` which pulled in `httpx`
during pytest collection and tripped the scan. Fix: push the
TestClient import inside each test body so the runtime contract
("trading bot never loads httpx") stays honest while still letting
the route tests use TestClient.

**Real dry-run against current disk**: confirmed the diagnosis -
BTC/ETH/SOL last 2025-12-31 (140 days stale), DXY 2026-05-15 (5
days, fresh). `freshness_status: stale_assets`. No assets missing
or empty.

**Tier preserved**: Tier-1 DIAGNOSTIC_ONLY / NOT_PROMOTABLE.
Trading PAUSED. Live BLOCKED.


## 2026-05-20 - Phase 5G close (5F-G-H combined arc)

**Decision**: Ship a Windows Task Scheduler integration that runs the
Phase 5F fresh-data update flow once per day at 21:15 local time.
Three PowerShell scripts: a daily runner that checks PAUSED.flag
before invoking the orchestrator, an installer that registers
exactly one named task pointing to the runner, and an uninstaller
that removes only that exact name. Also extend the orchestrator
itself with --update-dxy-fred (pinned FRED DTWEXBGS URL, curl.exe
--ssl-no-revoke download), --auto-start-from-last (next-day-after-
last per asset), and --force.

**Why**: The Phase 5F orchestrator was operator-run-only. The
operator does not want to type the command by hand every day.
Survive-reboot daily cadence is the natural next step, but only IF
every guardrail still holds. We delivered the cadence as a single
named Windows task whose action is a single PowerShell script whose
body invokes a single python tool with safe flags - and tests
statically enforce that contract.

**Why FRED DTWEXBGS proxy not exact ICE DXY**: DTWEXBGS is the
broad trade-weighted dollar index Freely available from FRED with no
API key and no auth surface. The operator already proved the
curl.exe --ssl-no-revoke download path works on this Windows host.
We label the staged asset DXY_PROXY_FRED_DTWEXBGS so no downstream
consumer mistakes it for the exact ICE DXY.

**Hard-boundary verifications (169 tests pass)**:
- The task action invokes ONLY run_shadow_validator_daily.ps1
  (variable-resolved in the installer; pinned by static test).
- The runner invokes ONLY the Phase 5F python orchestrator with a
  fixed safe-flag list. Tests assert disallowed flags
  (--execute / --trade / --place-order / --telegram / --webhook /
  --promote / --review-queue) are absent.
- The orchestrator source contains exactly one outbound URL token
  besides docstring references: the FRED DTWEXBGS URL. Any other
  URL passed to _assert_fred_dxy_url() raises.
- Tests assert no subprocess.run() in the orchestrator targets
  anything other than curl/curl.exe; no os.system / Popen.
- Tests assert no broker/order/execution/Telegram/webhook/Slack/
  review_queue/strategy_lab tokens appear in the active code of
  any PowerShell script (comments allowed for the deliberately-not-
  done contract).
- The PAUSED.flag check is asserted by static test against the
  runner script's source.

**Cross-test pollution carry-over**: The Phase 5F fix (lazy
TestClient import in route tests) continues to keep the Phase 5B
"runtime never loads httpx" scan honest.

**Operator-install commands**:
- Install: `powershell.exe -ExecutionPolicy Bypass -File tools\install_shadow_validator_task.ps1`
- Uninstall: `powershell.exe -ExecutionPolicy Bypass -File tools\uninstall_shadow_validator_task.ps1`

**Tier preserved**: Tier-1 DIAGNOSTIC_ONLY / NOT_PROMOTABLE.
Trading PAUSED. Live BLOCKED. No live trading or execution surface
was added.


## 2026-05-20 - Phase 5I close

**Decision**: Add ONE safe dashboard control - "Run Shadow Now" -
that triggers the non-executing fresh-data/shadow flow without
operator typing. The button POSTs to /shadow-validator/run-now; the
route delegates to a new ops launcher that invokes the canonical
PowerShell daily runner via subprocess.run with shell=False and a
hard-coded argv. PAUSED.flag and RUNNING.lock both short-circuit
the launch.

**Why**: The scheduled task is the right primary cadence, but the
operator also wanted a manual button on the dashboard for the case
"the task stalled" or "I just refreshed something and want one
immediate diagnostic run, now." Without this control, the only
manual paths were the CLI and clicking the Run option in Windows
Task Scheduler GUI - both clunky from the operator's workflow.

**Hard contract verified by tests (190 total pass)**:
- argv is hard-coded: ['powershell.exe', '-ExecutionPolicy',
  'Bypass', '-File', '<DAILY_RUNNER_PS1>']. No element is derived
  from operator input. The launcher's signature accepts no
  parameter that could carry a command fragment (asserted by
  inspect.signature scan).
- subprocess.run is always called with shell=False (asserted by
  static source scan with docstring stripping).
- The launcher refuses on PAUSED.flag (no lock written, no
  subprocess) and on a fresh RUNNING.lock (older than 35 min
  treated as stale crash debris).
- Lock is removed on both success and failure paths (asserted by
  tests that inject failing fake subprocess functions).
- latest_status.json is merged with manual_run_* fields on every
  attempt; existing scheduler/fresh-data fields are preserved.
- The new app.py block contains no broker/order/Telegram/webhook/
  scheduler-write/review_queue references (asserted by static scan
  scoped to the Phase 5I region of app.py).
- All four safety labels appear on the route response, lock
  payload, and updated status file.

**Cross-module monkeypatch lesson**: the test file imports the ops
module via the bare name `regime_shadow_ops`; the route imports it
as `tools.regime_shadow_ops`. These are TWO sys.modules entries.
Patching one does not affect the other. Tests now patch both when
the patched attribute needs to take effect inside the route.

**Tier preserved**: Tier-1 DIAGNOSTIC_ONLY / NOT_PROMOTABLE.
Trading PAUSED. Live BLOCKED. No live trading / execution surface
was added.


## 2026-05-20 - Phase 5K: Shadow Validation Decision Contract committed

**Decision**: Pre-commit to an objective stop / continue / redesign
contract for the shadow validator at Days 7 / 30 / 60 / 90 / 180.
File: reports/regime_intelligence/SPARTA_SHADOW_VALIDATION_DECISION_CONTRACT_20260520T234945Z.md
(+ .json machine-readable). Verdict enum: CONTINUE,
FIX_INFRASTRUCTURE, REDESIGN_SIGNAL, ARCHIVE_RESEARCH,
READY_FOR_PAPER_SIMULATION_DESIGN.

**Why**: After Phase 5K (the merge fix), the shadow validator
infrastructure is solid - 204 tests pass, the dashboard works, the
daily flow runs end to end. But infrastructure is not evidence. The
2025 historical replay showed -0.10% to -0.13% theoretical-vs-
benchmark across 1d/3d/7d - diagnostic, not predictive. Without a
pre-committed kill criterion, "let it run and see" can drift into
sunk-cost forever. The contract converts the next 6 months into a
real experiment with a real exit clause.

**Hard global kill conditions (any day, immediate ARCHIVE)**:
safety_audit_overall_pass == False, execution_surface_detected,
forbidden_language_found, any broker/order/Telegram/webhook/
review_queue surface, any modification to strategy_lab/ or
trading-bot/ or sparta_regime_intelligence core attributable to
the shadow flow.

**Cost proxy at Day 90 / Day 180**: 10 bps per active day applied
to theoretical returns when evaluating "after costs" verdicts.
NOT a real cost model - bounded conservative proxy only.

**Operator override policy**: may always override toward MORE
caution (e.g., ARCHIVE instead of CONTINUE). MAY NOT override
toward less caution. Tier-1 DIAGNOSTIC_ONLY / NOT_PROMOTABLE
preserved at every verdict including the best-case Day-180
READY_FOR_PAPER_SIMULATION_DESIGN (which itself would require a
separate explicit phase and is still NOT live trading).

- 2026-05-27 - DECISION - Framework-level DR10 SEAL revision INVESTIGATION
  plan authored as PLAN ONLY under operator authorization ('Authorize
  framework-level DR10 SEAL revision investigation PLAN only.'). This is
  Path T6 from the post-s13-d1 next-track selection plan. File written:
  `docs/framework_dr10_revision_investigation_plan_after_s13_d1_terminal
  .md` (507 lines; sha `450373a3c4fbc039058b1ff410dc4e92c95093e86028e254
  c580624458a04546`). No JSON sidecar; no canonical seal sha256 (PLAN-
  level investigation document, not a sealed Tier-N or framework SEAL).
  This document is NOT a SEAL revision; it scopes out what a future
  framework-level SEAL revision would need, presents math examples
  rigorously, and enumerates 7 governance options (A-G) without
  recommending any. Investigation question (formalized): is the current
  DR10 annual_turnover>0.50 threshold mathematically incompatible with
  K9 inviolate>=100 for active-trading strategies on liquid futures and
  cash equities at practical retail-scale start_cash ($100k-$1M)?
  Sub-Q1 answer (mathematically derived): NO compatibility at retail
  scale on liquid futures (contract-quantization forces per-trade
  notional >> 0.5% of start_cash); active cash-equity trading clears
  joint K9 + DR10 constraint only at unrealistic nano-sizing (0.005-
  0.02% risk per trade). Key derived constraint: per_trade_notional <=
  0.5% of start_cash to satisfy both K9 (OOS >=50 trades/y) AND DR10
  (annual_turnover <= 0.50). At $200k start_cash this means max
  per-trade notional <= $1,000 - infeasible for any liquid futures
  contract whose minimum unit notional ranges $20k (M2K) to $130k (6E).
  Cash equities at standard 0.5% risk produce 12-25x turnover at K9-
  clearing rates; only at 0.005-0.02% risk per trade do they clear DR10.
  Historical candidate audit: every actively-traded candidate in
  s9/s10/s11/s12/s13 lineage that progressed to IS execution had
  observed or estimated annual_turnover well above 0.50; the s13-d1
  outcome was the FIRST time DR10 was actually evaluated against
  observed annual_turnover because prior s11/s12-lineage candidates
  terminated at upstream gates (K9 inviolate, DR9 data integrity)
  before reaching P6.5. Implication: DR10's `annual_turnover>0.50`
  branch has been LATENT across the s9/s10/s11/s12 chain; s13-d1 first
  reached P6.5 with K9 cleared and edge positive, exposing the latent
  constraint. 7 governance options presented (each with math trade-offs,
  framework consequences, migration cost, defensibility): A status quo
  (no change), B raise threshold to calibrated higher value, C drop
  turnover branch keep S2_cost_drag only, D asset-class-specific
  threshold, E capital-scale-normalized threshold (counter-intuitive
  direction noted), F OR -> AND conjunction of branches (single-operator
  change), G defer. Critical clarification preserved across all options:
  per existing SEAL `no_dr_redefinition_post_seal=True` and
  `fail_safety_outcomes_terminal_for_this_candidate_record_id=True`,
  s13-d1's REJECT_FAST verdict and terminal lifecycle status are byte-
  equivalent and binding under the OLD DR10 regardless of which option
  is selected. A future SEAL revision (if any) applies ONLY to NEW SEAL
  turns going forward (s14+). Past sealed candidates retain their old
  DR10 verdicts byte-equivalent. SEAL revision scoping (NOT performed)
  documented in §8: fresh framework-level SEAL artifact at
  `reports/framework_dr10_revision_seal_v2.{json,md}`, audit trail
  explaining rationale, OLD vs NEW DR10 verdict tables for all prior
  candidates (informational, no verdict changes), revised DR-precedence
  chain consideration, migration rules, operator sign-off requirements.
  Boundaries held (PLAN-only document): no SEAL, no SEAL revision, no
  Tier-N spec, no DRAFT, no BUILD, no code, no backtest, no fetch, no
  Databento, no network, no live, no candidate promotion, no
  reinterpretation of DR10 in any existing sealed candidate, no
  modification of any existing sealed candidate artifact, no s13-d1 /
  s12-d1 / parked-candidate revival, no specific threshold proposal as

  `brain_memory/projects/trading_bot/lessons.md` modification or

## 2026-05-30 - Agentic Backtest Factory: Donchian + S26 + S27 + S28 ALL PARKED (consolidated decision record)

Consolidated final state of the isolated, offline-only, research-only validation pipeline at `trading_research/agentic_factory/`. Four strategy branches have now run through the manual validation ladder; none is deployable, paper-ready, or live-ready. OOS 2023-2025 remains SEALED on every parked branch.

- **Donchian branch — PARKED (reference baseline only):**
    - S23 = WATCH; S24 = ENTRY_EDGE_NOT_SUPPORTED; S25 = SEQUENCE_RISK_FRAGILE.
    - Final: useful reference baseline only — net flips negative without the top-3 winners; NOT deployable, NOT paper-ready.
- **S26 (Trend + Support/Resistance + EMA/RSI) — PARKED (strongest candidate so far, still parked):**
    - NQ OOS PASS; ES = PARTIAL_SUPPORT_WITH_CAUTION; entry edge = INCONCLUSIVE; regime risk = INCONCLUSIVE; walk-forward = INCONCLUSIVE; friction = SENSITIVE.
    - Final D18 decision: PARK_CANDIDATE. NOT paper-ready, NOT live-ready, NOT deployable.
- **S27 (Mean Reversion after Overextension in Bull Trend) — PARKED after IS_FAIL:**
    - Failed IS baseline: 18 trades, -1.7506R, PF 0.8372, negative expectancy. OOS 2023-2025 NOT touched.
- **S28 (Breakout-Retest + Volatility Expansion + Mechanical Bad-Regime Gate) — PARKED after IS_FAIL:**
    - Failed IS baseline: 12 trades, -0.72R net, PF 0.91, win rate 33.3%, expectancy -0.06R/trade, max DD 4.0R, positive years 3/10; exits 8 stops / 3 targets / 1 time stop.
    - Total R without top-3 winners = -6.72R; anti-Donchian top-3 gate = FAIL. Every pre-registered IS hard floor breached. OOS 2023-2025 NOT touched.
    - S28-D4 IS_FAIL decision-record commit: full `1ef71fe5fe7e7db08adabec0625ec7a915898b35`, short `1ef71fe` (committed exactly 2 files: report.json + report.md; e7ce9a9 remains ancestor; no source/engine/test/data committed; JARVIS commit bdcca5a touched no agentic_factory file).
- **Validation tooling now proven/in-use (the manual ladder):** pre-registered frozen strategy specs · IS baseline · OOS-protocol-before-OOS · one-shot OOS · entry significance (vs random AND vs raw breakout) · Monte Carlo / sequence risk · regime breakdown · multi-market robustness · walk-forward stability · friction/slippage stress · risk/readiness gate · final park/promote decision records · explicit-pathspec commit method to avoid JARVIS index-race contamination.
- **Recommendation:** PARK S28. Do NOT create or run S28-D5 OOS. Do NOT optimize/re-tune any parked branch in place (anti-overfit). Donchian, S26, S27 remain PARKED.

- 2026-06-01 — **Decision (Next Bundle Generator v1, Bundle 2):** Built `tools/strategy_next_bundle.py` — a stdlib-only, research-only, deterministic generator that reads Routine Layer outputs (`strategy_queue/queue.json`, `daily_state/latest_state.json`, `weekly_review/latest_weekly_review.json`, `storage/jarvis/strategy_factory/latest_strategy_factory_snapshot.json`) and writes `next_bundle.json` / `.md` / `next_claude_prompt.txt` into a new gitignored runtime folder `reports/strategy_factory_routines/next_bundle/`. CLI: `generate / show / validate`. Selection filters out `blocked=True`, non-`research_only` safety levels, and any item containing broker/live/paper-order/credential/scheduler danger keywords (defense in depth); scores on priority + weekly/daily lane alignment + protocol-first/data-first/copy-paste-reducing/validation/edge hints, with deterministic tiebreak (score desc → lane → title). Pinned-False trading flags asserted in JSON and validated by the `validate` command. Tests: `tests/test_strategy_next_bundle.py` (19 passing). Trackable docs at `reports/strategy_factory_next_bundle_generator/`. `lessons.md` NOT touched. No commit made (awaiting approval).

- 2026-06-01 — **Decision (Strategy Candidate Registry v1, Bundle 3):** Built `tools/strategy_candidate_registry.py` — a stdlib-only, research-only, deterministic registry of every SPARTA strategy/lane (CRYPTO D1/4H, NQ/ES futures trend, Donchian variants, vol-confirmed continuation, arbitrage protocol, data QA/freeze, JARVIS automation, Strategy Factory infra). Scans `trading_research/agentic_factory/reports/` folder/file names and applies conservative substring rules to classify each seed lane (`failed_`/`rejected`→FAILED, `retire`→RETIRED, `park`/`closeout`→PARKED, `block`→BLOCKED, `watch`/`oos_result`→WATCH, `*baseline*`→ACTIVE, `spec`/`protocol`/`plan`→IDEA) with the most-severe-wins precedence. Hard guardrail: auto-build never emits `evidence_level=STRONG`. CLI: `build / show / validate`. Output `candidates.json` / `candidates.md` in a new gitignored folder `reports/strategy_factory_routines/candidate_registry/`. Next Bundle Generator updated to optionally read the registry: filters out `FAILED`/`RETIRED` lanes from the queue and bonus-scores `ACTIVE` (+25) / `WATCH` (+15). Tests: `tests/test_strategy_candidate_registry.py` (16 passing) + 5 new registry-integration tests in `tests/test_strategy_next_bundle.py` (24/24 passing). Trackable docs at `reports/strategy_candidate_registry_v1/`. `lessons.md` NOT touched. `app.py` / `templates/jarvis.html` NOT touched. No commit made (awaiting approval).
